 amitabh aisa naam he, jinhen aaj kii yuva peedi hi nahin, balki aane vaali kai peediyaan apana adarsh maan sakati hai
 He had to go through a struggle to become a prominent figure in the history of Indian cinema
 unhen apane kariyar kii shuruyaat main kai uphaas sahane pade
 He had to lose a few films because of his tall stature
 unki awaaj ko lekar bhi majaak udaaya gaya
 'whenever the world laughed at him, then history is created', he made it come true
 lanbaa kad or buland aawaaj unhen sabase khaas banaati he
 He has also lent his voice to someone else in Bollywood like 'babul'
 kehete hai ki kaagaj apni kismat se udata he, lekin patang apni kabaliyat se udati he
 Friends, Amitabh ji can be called a kite, because he conquered the world with his success
 amitabh bachchan kii shaadi abhinetri jaya bhadudi se hui
 She first met him at the Film and Television Institute in Pune
 amitabh kii ek beti shweta nanda or betaa abhishek bachchan hai
 Both are married
 amitabh kaa ek naati, ek nathin or ek potee aradhya bhi he
 In Hindi cinema, Abhinabh starred in 'zanjeer', 'roti Kapad Aur Makaan', 'khuda Witness', 'kuli', 'kunwara Bap', 'farrar', 'sholay', 'chupke Chupke', 'kasme Vaade', 'trishul' ',' Muqaddar ka Sikandar ',' Mr
 natvarlaal', 'kaala pathar', 'dostana', 'silsilaa', 'shaan', 'laavaaris' or 'shakti' jaisi mashhoor filmon main kaam kiya
 Apart from this, he also made the audience crazy with many reality shows like 'kaun Banega Crorepati'
 amitabh ne apane kariyar main kai uplabdhiyaan hasil kii hai
 He made a lot of headlines during his lifetime
 vah abhinetri rekha ke saath rishte ko lekar bhi charchaa main rahe
 It is said that Rekha wanted Amitabh in his heart, but Amitabh never moved forward with this relationship
 tippaniyan Youngsters can cherish dreams of moving forward in life with their ideals, because no one can tell when, where, and how their times will change
 jis tarah amitabh ne apane jivan ke kaanton ko paar kar aisi jagah ja pahunche, jisase vah sabhi kii ankhon kaa tara ban gaye hai, vaise hi hamen bhi jivan main unke udhaaharan lekar kathin se kathin raah ko chunakar use paar karnaa chahie
 Lakhs of thorns may come in the way, but your feet do not waver, this inspires the struggling life of the great
 amitabh bachchan ke sangharsh or safalataa kii kahani jitani ascharyajanak he, utani hi romaanchak bhi, jitani avishwasaneey he, utani hi sammohak bhi
 Amitabh has turned 72 years old today, but the passion to work in him can be seen even today
 vah aaj bhi kaam ko lekar utane hi utsahit hai
 Amitabh was born on 11 October 1942 in Allahabad, Uttar Pradesh
 bachchan kysth parivaar se sambandh rakhte hai
 Famous Hindi poet Dr
 harivansh raay bachchan unke pita the
 His mother Teji Bachchan had a keen interest in theater, yet he preferred to handle the house
 saal 2003 main amitabh ke sir se pita kaa saaya uth gaya, jabaki unki maa ne 21 disambar 2007 ko unhen alavida kaha
 He always had a deep affection for his mother
 amitabh kaa arth he 'kabhi na bujhane vaali lau' or unhone apane naam kaa arth sarthak kar dikhaaya
 Amitabh is such a name, which not only the young generation of today, but many generations to come, can consider their ideal
 unhen bhartiya cinema ke itihaas main pramukh vyakti banane ke liye sangharsh ke daur se guzarana padaa
 He had to endure many ridicule in the beginning of his career
 unhen kuch filmon se to sirf unke lambey kad kii vajah se haath dhonaa padaa
 His voice was also mocked
 'jab-jab jag us par hansaa he, tab tab itihaas rachaa he' unhone yah sach kar dikhaaya
 His tall stature and lofty voice make him most special
 unhone bollywood main 'babul' jaisi film main kisi duusare ko apni aawaaj bhi di he
 It is said that paper flies by its luck, but kite flies with its ability
 doston amitabh ji ko patang kaha ja saktaa he, kyonki unhone apni kamyaabi se duniya ko jeet liya
 Amitabh Bachchan is married to actress Jaya Bhaduri
 unase unki pehali mulaakaat pune ke film and televijan institute main hui thi
 Amitabh has a daughter Shweta Nanda and son Abhishek Bachchan
 donon kii shaadi ho gai he
 Amitabh also has a grandson, a granddaughter and a granddaughter, Aaradhya
 abhitabh ne hindi cinema main 'zanjeer', 'roti kapadaa or makaan', 'khuda gavaah', 'kuli', 'kunvaara baap', 'faraar', 'sholay', 'chupake chupake', 'kasame vaade', 'trishul', 'mukaddar kaa sikandar', 'mi
 Worked in famous films like Natwarlal ',' Kala Patthar ',' Dostana ',' Silsila ',' Shaan ',' Lavaris' and 'shakti'
 iske alaava unhone 'koun banegaa karodpati' jaise kai reality sho se bhi darshakon ko apana divaana banaaya
 Amitabh has achieved many achievements in his career
 unhone apane jeevankaal main khub surkhiyaan batorin
 He was also in the discussion regarding the relationship with actress Rekha
 bataaya jaataa he ki rekha dil hi dil main amitabh ko chaahati thim, lekin amitabh kabhi is rishte ko lekar aage nahin bade
 The comments yuva unke aadarshon ko lekar jivan main aage badhane ke sapane sanjo sakate hai, kyonki vakt kab, kahaan, kiskaa kaise badal jaae yah koi nahin bataa saktaa

 Liam Thomas's fake leg while fielding turned out to be a T20 match between physically challenged people between England and Pakistan in Dubai
 jahaan england ke fielder liyaan thomas becoward scoir leg par fielding kar rahe the

 chaunsath sutara solah abhimaan 'kamasutra' se prerit kavy sangrah he

 is sangrah main shaamil kavitaayen ek lambii kavita ke do khandon ke alag-alag charnon ke rup main prastut kii gai hai

 vatsyayan krit kamasutra

 kavi prem or kaamrat premi bhi rahata he or drushtaakavi bhi

 ) shivasena or bijepi gathbandhan main ek baar phir daraar aa gai he

 bhale hi donon partiyon ke netaa is maamle main ek duusare par aarope-pratyarope kar rahe hon, lekin iske raajnneetik myne kuch or hi hai

 shivasena desh kii sabase badi kahe jane vaale west coast oil rifynary project ke khilaaf pradarshan kar rahi he
 In this regard, Shiv Sena supremo Uddhav Thackeray said that we will not allow the refinery project to be put up in Konkan, as it will harm the environment
 yahi nahin, project nanar gaanv ke logon ke khilaaf he
 If this project takes place, outsiders will buy the land of the people of the village
 thakare is project ko lekar pradhanmantri narendra modi or mukhyamantri devendra fadanvis ko saaf shabdon main yah chetavanee de chuke hai ki wo is project ke khilaaf he or yadi ise sarkaar lagaana chaahati he to vidarbha yaa phir gujarat main lagaae
 How is the project
 
 
 ab project kii baat kii jaae to is rifynary kii prastaavit kshamta 60 million ton prati varsh hogi
 That means 70 percent more than India's largest refinery in Jamnagar at present
 philhal jamnagar rifynary kii kshamta 35 million ton he
 The project cost three lakh crores
 
 
 is project kii laagat teen lakh karod rupee he
 If this project is completed, it will provide employment to one lakh people
 rifynary ko philhal teen public sector pramot karenge
 These are Hindustan Petroleum (HPCL), Bharat Petroleum (BPCL) and Indian Oil (IOC)
 in teenon main sabase bada partner he indian oil
 It has a 50% stake in the project
 vahiin, hindustan petroleum or bharat petroleum kii hissedari 25 % he
 On April 11, 2018, an mou was signed between the three psus and Saudi Aramco to build the refinery and petrochemicals complex
 iske baad 2015 main centre sarkaar ne project lagane ke liye maharashtra ko chunaa
 What does the BJP have to say on Shiv Sena's allegations? BJP says that the environmental damage caused by this project is completely wrong
 yah ek green project he or isamen advance technology kaa istemaal hoga, jo paryaavaran ko nuksaan nahin pahunchayegaa
 The BJP also raised the question that the Shiv Sena never protested when nuclear projects were set up in Maharashtra
 phir ab is project par kyon adanga laga rahe hai

 to aakhir kya he iske peeche raajnneeti?bijepi adhyaksh amit shahne 2019 main hone vaale loksabhaa chunaav main shivasena ke saath dobaaraa chunaav ladane kii baat kahi thi, lekin shivasena netaaon ne is mudde se kinaaraa kar liya

 lekin konkan ko lekar raajnneeti kuch or hi he

 jabaki yahaan bijepi lambey samay se pair pasaarne kii koshish kar rahi he
